      <h2 class="main-section-heading h-c-headline h-c-headline--two underline-blue"><span class="focus-hijack">Keep customers informed</span></h2> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <div class="persona-submodule-wrapper h-c-grid"> 
     <div class="links-module h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col-s--4 h-c-grid__col-l--5 h-c-grid__col-l--offset-1 h-c-grid__col--align-middle"> 
      <div class="links-copy-section"> 
       <h3 class="h-c-headline h-c-headline--three section-headline" unite-orphan="">Claim or update your Business Profile for free.</h3>
       <p>As your business goes through different phases of lockdown and reopening, it’s even more important to be found online and provide updated information to potential customers. A <a href="https://business.google.com/create?gmbsrc=us-en_US-et-gs-z-gmb-s-z-u~sb-g4sb-u&amp;ppsrc=GMBB0&amp;utm_campaign=us-en_US-et-gs-z-gmb-s-z-u~sb-g4sb-u&amp;utm_source=gmb&amp;utm_medium=et&amp;gmbsrc=us-en_US-et-gs-z-gmb-s-z-u~sb-g4sb-u-WLC-CVH-INL" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-referral-tracking="" data-position="c19-v4-gmb">Business Profile</a> on Google will help you show up on Google Search and Maps. Once you claim your profile, you can add photos, post updates, adjust your business hours, and more.</p>

      <div class="links-copy-section"> 
       <h3 class="h-c-headline h-c-headline--three section-headline" unite-orphan="">Create or optimize your website</h3>
       <p>To help you get discovered online and showcase your business, you’ll want to create a website and start with a unique web address. (Don’t worry, there are website builders for all skill levels.) Drive traffic by adding your website address to your Business Profile.</p>

      <h2 class="main-section-heading h-c-headline h-c-headline--two underline-yellow"><span class="focus-hijack">Work remotely</span></h2> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <div class="persona-submodule-wrapper h-c-grid"> 
     <div class="links-module h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col-s--4 h-c-grid__col-l--5 h-c-grid__col-l--offset-1 h-c-grid__col--align-middle"> 
      <div class="links-copy-section"> 
       <h3 class="h-c-headline h-c-headline--three section-headline" unite-orphan="">Run your business remotely</h3>
       <p>There are many tools to help you and your team stay connected and productive from afar. You can collaborate on docs; easily store and access them on the cloud; and have safe, secure video conferences with customers, no matter where you are.</p>

      <h2 class="main-section-heading h-c-headline h-c-headline--two underline-green"><span class="focus-hijack">Reach more customers</span></h2> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <div class="persona-submodule-wrapper h-c-grid"> 
     <div class="links-module image-left h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col-s--4 h-c-grid__col-l--5 h-c-grid__col-l--offset-1 h-c-grid__col-xl--5 h-c-grid__col-xl--offset-1 h-c-grid__col--align-middle"> 
      <div class="links-copy-section"> 
       <h3 class="h-c-headline h-c-headline--three section-headline" unite-orphan="">Adjust your advertising or get started with Ads</h3>
       <p class="h-c-copy">Getting in front of new customers can be particularly challenging during COVID-19, however, with <a href="https://ads.google.com/home/?subid=us-en-et-g-aw-a-g4sb_1!o2-WLC-CVH-INL" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-referral-tracking="" data-position="c19-v4-ads">Google Ads</a>, you can get your business to appear at the exact moment people are searching for what you offer. Set a monthly budget that works for you and never go over it.</p>

      <h2 class="main-section-heading h-c-headline h-c-headline--two underline-yellow"><span class="focus-hijack">Explore financial assistance</span></h2> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <div class="h-c-grid"> 
     <div class="h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col-s--4 h-c-grid__col--8 h-c-grid__col--offset-2 h-c-grid__col-xl--6 h-c-grid__col-xl--offset-3"> 
      <h3 class="h-c-headline h-c-headline--three carousel-heading" unite-orphan="">Loans and grants from the government</h3> 
      <p class="h-c-copy carousel-subheading" unite-orphan="">We've compiled a list of up-to-date, government-supported financial programs that are still accepting applications from small business owners impacted by COVID-19.</p>
